Lines is a game play on 9×9 board with balls of seven different colors. The object is to connect 5 or more balls of the same color to a horizontal, vertical or diagonal line. \r\nThe player can move one ball per turn, and the player may only move a ball to a particular place if there is a path (linked set of vertical and horizontal empty cells) between the current position of the ball and the desired destination.
